        </tr>

          <td id="L355" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="355"></td>
          <td id="LC355" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">To find where your true image pictured lies,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L356" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="356"></td>
          <td id="LC356" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Which in my bosom&#39;s shop is hanging still,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L357" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="357"></td>
          <td id="LC357" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">That hath his windows glazed with thine eyes:</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L358" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="358"></td>
          <td id="LC358" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Now see what good turns eyes for eyes have done,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L359" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="359"></td>
          <td id="LC359" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Mine eyes have drawn thy shape, and thine for me</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L360" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="360"></td>
          <td id="LC360" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Are windows to my breast, where-through the sun</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L361" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="361"></td>
          <td id="LC361" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Delights to peep, to gaze therein on thee;  </td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L362" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="362"></td>
          <td id="LC362" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Yet eyes this cunning want to grace their art,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L363" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="363"></td>
          <td id="LC363" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">They draw but what they see, know not the heart.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L364" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="364"></td>
          <td id="LC364" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L365" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="365"></td>
          <td id="LC365" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Let those who are in favour with their stars,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L366" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="366"></td>
          <td id="LC366" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Of public honour and proud titles boast,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L367" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="367"></td>
          <td id="LC367" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Whilst I whom fortune of such triumph bars</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L368" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="368"></td>
          <td id="LC368" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Unlooked for joy in that I honour most;</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L369" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="369"></td>
          <td id="LC369" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Great princes&#39; favourites their fair leaves spread,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L370" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="370"></td>
          <td id="LC370" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">But as the marigold at the sun&#39;s eye,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L371" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="371"></td>
          <td id="LC371" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">And in themselves their pride lies buried,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L372" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="372"></td>
          <td id="LC372" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">For at a frown they in their glory die.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L373" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="373"></td>
          <td id="LC373" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The painful warrior famoused for fight,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L374" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="374"></td>
          <td id="LC374" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">After a thousand victories once foiled,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L375" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="375"></td>
          <td id="LC375" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Is from the book of honour razed quite,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L376" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="376"></td>
          <td id="LC376" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">And all the rest forgot for which he toiled:</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L377" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="377"></td>
          <td id="LC377" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Then happy I that love and am beloved</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L378" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="378"></td>
          <td id="LC378" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Where I may not remove nor be removed.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L379" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="379"></td>
          <td id="LC379" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">  </td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L380" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="380"></td>
          <td id="LC380" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Lord of my love, to whom in vassalage</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L381" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="381"></td>
          <td id="LC381" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Thy merit hath my duty strongly knit;</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L382" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="382"></td>
          <td id="LC382" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">To thee I send this written embassage</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L383" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="383"></td>
          <td id="LC383" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">To witness duty, not to show my wit.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L384" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="384"></td>
          <td id="LC384" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Duty so great, which wit so poor as mine</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L385" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="385"></td>
          <td id="LC385" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">May make seem bare, in wanting words to show it;</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L386" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="386"></td>
          <td id="LC386" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">But that I hope some good conceit of thine</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L387" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="387"></td>
          <td id="LC387" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In thy soul&#39;s thought (all naked) will bestow it:</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L388" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="388"></td>
          <td id="LC388" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Till whatsoever star that guides my moving,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L389" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="389"></td>
          <td id="LC389" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Points on me graciously with fair aspect,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L390" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="390"></td>
          <td id="LC390" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">And puts apparel on my tattered loving,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L391" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="391"></td>
          <td id="LC391" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">To show me worthy of thy sweet respect,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L392" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="392"></td>
          <td id="LC392" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Then may I dare to boast how I do love thee,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L393" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="393"></td>
          <td id="LC393" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Till then, not show my head where thou mayst prove me.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L394" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="394"></td>
          <td id="LC394" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L395" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="395"></td>
          <td id="LC395" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Weary with toil, I haste me to my bed,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L396" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="396"></td>
          <td id="LC396" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The dear respose for limbs with travel tired,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L397" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="397"></td>
          <td id="LC397" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">But then begins a journey in my head</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L398" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="398"></td>
          <td id="LC398" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">To work my mind, when body&#39;s work&#39;s expired.  </td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L399" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="399"></td>
          <td id="LC399" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">For then my thoughts (from far where I abide)</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L400" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="400"></td>
          <td id="LC400" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Intend a zealous pilgrimage to thee,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L401" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="401"></td>
          <td id="LC401" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">And keep my drooping eyelids open wide,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L402" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="402"></td>
          <td id="LC402" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Looking on darkness which the blind do see.</td>

        <tr>
          <td id="L403" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="403"></td>
          <td id="LC403" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Save that my soul&#39;s imaginary sight</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L404" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="404"></td>
          <td id="LC404" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Presents thy shadow to my sightless view,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L405" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="405"></td>
          <td id="LC405" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Which like a jewel (hung in ghastly night)</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L406" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="406"></td>
          <td id="LC406" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Makes black night beauteous, and her old face new.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L407" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="407"></td>
          <td id="LC407" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Lo thus by day my limbs, by night my mind,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L408" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="408"></td>
          <td id="LC408" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">For thee, and for my self, no quiet find.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L409" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="409"></td>
          <td id="LC409" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L410" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="410"></td>
          <td id="LC410" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">How can I then return in happy plight</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L411" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="411"></td>
          <td id="LC411" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">That am debarred the benefit of rest?</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L412" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="412"></td>
          <td id="LC412" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">When day&#39;s oppression is not eased by night,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>

          <td id="LC413" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">But day by night and night by day oppressed.</td>

          <td id="L414" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="414"></td>
          <td id="LC414" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">And each (though enemies to either&#39;s reign)</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L415" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="415"></td>
          <td id="LC415" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Do in consent shake hands to torture me,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L416" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="416"></td>
          <td id="LC416" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The one by toil, the other to complain</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L417" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="417"></td>
          <td id="LC417" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">How far I toil, still farther off from thee.  </td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L418" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="418"></td>
          <td id="LC418" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">I tell the day to please him thou art bright,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L419" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="419"></td>
          <td id="LC419" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">And dost him grace when clouds do blot the heaven:</td>

          <td id="L421" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="421"></td>
          <td id="LC421" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">When sparkling stars twire not thou gild&#39;st the even.</td>

          <td id="LC422" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">But day doth daily draw my sorrows longer,</td>

</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L425" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="425"></td>
          <td id="LC425" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">When in disgrace with Fortune and men&#39;s eyes,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L426" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="426"></td>
          <td id="LC426" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">I all alone beweep my outcast state,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L427" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="427"></td>
          <td id="LC427" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">And trouble deaf heaven with my bootless cries,</td>

          <td id="LC428" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">And look upon my self and curse my fate,</td>

          <td id="L429" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="429"></td>
          <td id="LC429" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Wishing me like to one more rich in hope,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L430" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="430"></td>
          <td id="LC430" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Featured like him, like him with friends possessed,</td>

        <tr>
          <td id="L431" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="431"></td>
          <td id="LC431" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Desiring this man&#39;s art, and that man&#39;s scope,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L432" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="432"></td>
          <td id="LC432" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">With what I most enjoy contented least,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L433" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="433"></td>
          <td id="LC433" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Yet in these thoughts my self almost despising,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L434" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="434"></td>
          <td id="LC434" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Haply I think on thee, and then my state,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L435" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="435"></td>
          <td id="LC435" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">(Like to the lark at break of day arising</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L436" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="436"></td>
          <td id="LC436" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">From sullen earth) sings hymns at heaven&#39;s gate,  </td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L437" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="437"></td>
          <td id="LC437" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">For thy sweet love remembered such wealth brings,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L438" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="438"></td>
          <td id="LC438" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">That then I scorn to change my state with kings.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L439" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="439"></td>

</td>

        <tr>

          <td id="LC440" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">When to the sessions of sweet silent thought,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L441" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="441"></td>
          <td id="LC441" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">I summon up remembrance of things past,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L442" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="442"></td>
          <td id="LC442" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">I sigh the lack of many a thing I sought,</td>

        <tr>
          <td id="L443" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="443"></td>
          <td id="LC443" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">And with old woes new wail my dear time&#39;s waste:</td>

          <td id="LC444" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Then can I drown an eye (unused to flow)</td>

        <tr>
          <td id="L445" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="445"></td>
          <td id="LC445" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">For precious friends hid in death&#39;s dateless night,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L446" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="446"></td>
          <td id="LC446" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">And weep afresh love&#39;s long since cancelled woe,</td>

          <td id="LC448" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Then can I grieve at grievances foregone,</td>

        </tr>

          <td id="LC608" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">When I am sometime absent from thy heart,</td>

        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2418" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2418"></td>
          <td id="LC2418" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">He is contented thy poor drudge to be,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2419" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2419"></td>
          <td id="LC2419" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">To stand in thy affairs, fall by thy side.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2420" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2420"></td>
          <td id="LC2420" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">No want of conscience hold it that I call,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2421" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2421"></td>
          <td id="LC2421" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Her love, for whose dear love I rise and fall.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2422" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2422"></td>
          <td id="LC2422" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2423" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2423"></td>
          <td id="LC2423" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In loving thee thou know&#39;st I am forsworn,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2424" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2424"></td>
          <td id="LC2424" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">But thou art twice forsworn to me love swearing,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2425" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2425"></td>
          <td id="LC2425" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In act thy bed-vow broke and new faith torn,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2426" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2426"></td>
          <td id="LC2426" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In vowing new hate after new love bearing:</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2427" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2427"></td>
          <td id="LC2427" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">But why of two oaths&#39; breach do I accuse thee,  </td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2428" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2428"></td>
          <td id="LC2428" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">When I break twenty? I am perjured most,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2429" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2429"></td>
          <td id="LC2429" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">For all my vows are oaths but to misuse thee:</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2430" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2430"></td>
          <td id="LC2430" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">And all my honest faith in thee is lost.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2431" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2431"></td>
          <td id="LC2431" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">For I have sworn deep oaths of thy deep kindness:</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2432" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2432"></td>
          <td id="LC2432" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Oaths of thy love, thy truth, thy constancy,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2433" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2433"></td>
          <td id="LC2433" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">And to enlighten thee gave eyes to blindness,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2434" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2434"></td>
          <td id="LC2434" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Or made them swear against the thing they see.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2435" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2435"></td>
          <td id="LC2435" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">For I have sworn thee fair: more perjured I,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2436" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2436"></td>
          <td id="LC2436" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">To swear against the truth so foul a be.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2437" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2437"></td>
          <td id="LC2437" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2438" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2438"></td>
          <td id="LC2438" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Cupid laid by his brand and fell asleep,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2439" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2439"></td>
          <td id="LC2439" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">A maid of Dian&#39;s this advantage found,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2440" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2440"></td>
          <td id="LC2440" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">And his love-kindling fire did quickly steep</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2441" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2441"></td>
          <td id="LC2441" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">In a cold valley-fountain of that ground:</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2442" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2442"></td>
          <td id="LC2442" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Which borrowed from this holy fire of Love,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2443" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2443"></td>
          <td id="LC2443" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">A dateless lively heat still to endure,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2444" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2444"></td>
          <td id="LC2444" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">And grew a seeting bath which yet men prove,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2445" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2445"></td>
          <td id="LC2445" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Against strange maladies a sovereign cure:</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2446" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2446"></td>
          <td id="LC2446" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">But at my mistress&#39; eye Love&#39;s brand new-fired,  </td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2447" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2447"></td>
          <td id="LC2447" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The boy for trial needs would touch my breast,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2448" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2448"></td>
          <td id="LC2448" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">I sick withal the help of bath desired,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2449" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2449"></td>
          <td id="LC2449" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">And thither hied a sad distempered guest.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2450" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2450"></td>
          <td id="LC2450" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">But found no cure, the bath for my help lies,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2451" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2451"></td>
          <td id="LC2451" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Where Cupid got new fire; my mistress&#39; eyes.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2452" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2452"></td>
          <td id="LC2452" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2453" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2453"></td>
          <td id="LC2453" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The little Love-god lying once asleep,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2454" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2454"></td>
          <td id="LC2454" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Laid by his side his heart-inflaming brand,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2455" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2455"></td>
          <td id="LC2455" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Whilst many nymphs that vowed chaste life to keep,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2456" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2456"></td>
          <td id="LC2456" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Came tripping by, but in her maiden hand,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2457" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2457"></td>
          <td id="LC2457" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">The fairest votary took up that fire,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2458" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2458"></td>
          <td id="LC2458" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Which many legions of true hearts had warmed,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2459" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2459"></td>
          <td id="LC2459" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">And so the general of hot desire,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2460" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2460"></td>
          <td id="LC2460" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Was sleeping by a virgin hand disarmed.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2461" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2461"></td>
          <td id="LC2461" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">This brand she quenched in a cool well by,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2462" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2462"></td>
          <td id="LC2462" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Which from Love&#39;s fire took heat perpetual,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2463" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2463"></td>
          <td id="LC2463" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Growing a bath and healthful remedy,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2464" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2464"></td>
          <td id="LC2464" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">For men discased, but I my mistress&#39; thrall,</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2465" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2465"></td>
          <td id="LC2465" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Came there for cure and this by that I prove,  </td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2466" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2466"></td>
          <td id="LC2466" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">Love&#39;s fire heats water, water cools not love.</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2467" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2467"></td>
          <td id="LC2467" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2468" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2468"></td>
          <td id="LC2468" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">
</td>
        </tr>
        <tr>
          <td id="L2469" class="blob-num js-line-number js-code-nav-line-number js-blob-rnum" data-line-number="2469"></td>
          <td id="LC2469" class="blob-code blob-code-inner js-file-line">                THE END</td>
        </tr>
  </table>
